romanian russian slovak spanish swedish turkish updated june 11 2021 this cookie notice describes how honeywell international inc and its affiliates collectively honeywell us or we use cookies and similar technologies installed on devices such as a computer mobile device or tablet devices of the visitors to or users of our website products andor applications sites cookies and similar technologies may process personal information please visit our privacy statement if you want to obtain more information about how we process your personal information and how to exercise your data subject rights our privacy preference center for more information on the specific cookies we use on our sites and to manage your cookie preferences what are cookies cookies are small text files that our sites place on your devices when you revisit our sites our technologies connect automatically with the cookie to identify you or your device and recall information about you such as your language preference or login information we also use thirdparty cookies which are cookies from a domain different than the domain of the website you are visiting which allow us the third party that owns the cookies and in some cases other participants in cookie networks to identify you or your device as you visit different websites we use the word cookies to include a piece of text pixels clear gifs log files web beacons or other similar tracking technology that are placed on your devices there are four types of cookies that we may use strictly necessary cookies are needed for our sites to function and to provide you with the services and information that you have requested strictly necessary cookies are exempt from the consent requirement functional cookies enable enhanced functionality and personalisation for example they allow our sites to remember information that you provide such as your language preferences and to store technical information useful for your interactions with our sites they may be set by us or by thirdparty providers whose services we have added to our sites if you do not allow these cookies then some or all of these services may not function properly performance cookies collect information about your use of our sites for eg it allows us to count visits and traffic sources and help us learn how our sites are performing so that we can make relevant improvements that could better your browsing experience for eg it allow us to know which pages are the most and least popular all information these cookies collect is aggregated and therefore anonymous advertising targeting cookies collect data about your online activity and identify your interests so that we can create a profile for you and to provide advertising that is more relevant to you they also perform functions like preventing the same adverts from continuously reappearing ensuring that adverts are properly displayed and selecting adverts that are based on your interests for more information on the cookies that honeywell uses please visit our privacy preference center why do we use cookies and other similar technologies we use cookies and other similar tracking technologies for the following purposes store your preferences and settings permit you to signin and authenticate you so that you can access our sites and to move from page to page within our sites secure our sites including fraud detection and prevention tailor information presented to you based on your browsing preferences such as language and geographical region monitor the traffic patterns of users within our sites and to collect statistics regarding your website usage to help us understand how our sites perform and how we can improve our sites for purposes such as enhancing your browsing experience and offering services that are more relevant to you provide us with business and marketing information track users who visit interact with or use any of our sites social media pages online advertisements and marketing communications such as which adverts where clicked on or if a user has opened or forwarded an email we have sent them and targeted advertising and crossdevice and crosssite tracking who uses the information stored in cookies and similar tracking technologies the information stored in our sites cookies is used exclusively by us or by third parties acting on our behalf with the exception of thirdparty cookies which are used and managed by external parties to provide services requested by us to improve our services and your experience when navigating our sites for more information on the firstparty and thirdparty cookies that honeywell uses please visit our privacy preference center what about flash cookies or local shared objects we may use flash cookies or local shared objects flash lsos to store your website preferences personalise your visit prevent fraud and for other site operations if you do not want flash lsos stored on your computer you can adjust the settings of your flash player to block flash lsos storage using the tools contained in the website storage settings panel you can also control flash lsos by going to the global storage settings panel and following the instructions which may include instructions that explain for example how to delete existing flash lsos targeted advertising we track and analyse both individualized usage and aggregated statistical information related to your use of our sites we also partner with third parties such as advertisers and ad partners to display advertising on our sites and to manage and serve advertising on other thirdparty sites these third parties use cookies and similar tracking technologies to collect and use certain information about your online activities either on our sites or other thirdparty sites to measure and track the effectiveness of advertisements and our online marketing activities for example by collecting data on how many times you click on one of our advertisements this information may be used alone or in combination with information about you we obtain from other sources like our data partners your contact details and honeywell transaction history to infer your interests and deliver you targeted advertisements and marketing that are more tailored to you based on your browsing activities and inferred interests interestbased advertising such interestbased advertising will only be delivered where permitted by applicable law and in accordance with your advertisingmarketing preferences please note that other third parties cookies and technologies are governed by each companys specific privacy policy and not this cookie notice crossdevice and crosssite tracking we our service providers and other third parties such as google and other ad partners may use information we collect about you whether directly from our sites or from a third party for the purposes of recognizing you online by identifying the devices that you use we use this information to serve you targeted advertising across multiple different devices crossdevice matching and sites crosssite tracking crossdevice matching and crosssite tracking allows us to better understand our customers activity improve our ability to target and measure ad campaigns including limiting the number of times a user sees an advert it also helps us match devices so we can facilitate your optout choices across all the devices we know are connected to an optedout cookie disabling cookies and opting out of interestbased advertising you can make choices about receiving cookies by using our privacy preference center or alternatively your browser settings should allow you to delete andor disable website cookies for more information about how to delete your cookies in your web browser refer to your browsers instructions google chrome internet explorer microsoft edge mozilla firefox opera safari mac iphone ipad or ipod touch if you choose to disable cookies you may find sites may not work in the same way some cookies are necessary to record and respect the choices you have made in regard to not being contacted or to not have other types of cookies added to your device if you delete cookies from your computer the cookie used to recognize your preferences including interestbased advertising will also be deleted requiring you to make your choices again users may also opt out of thirdparty ad networks through the use of various trade association websites such as network advertising initiative nai httpwwwnetworkadvertisingorgchoices digital advertising our partners if at any time you do not want your personal information to be used to allow thirdparties to display advertisements or to personalize advertisements displayed to you you may also adjust was sind cookies cookies sind kleine textdateien die unsere websites auf ihren gerten ablegen wenn sie unsere websites erneut besuchen stellen unsere technologien automatisch eine verbindung mit dem cookie her um sie oder ihr gert zu identifizieren und informationen zu ihnen abzurufen z b ihre spracheinstellungen oder anmeldeinformationen darber hinaus verwenden wir cookies von drittanbietern andere hnliche nachverfolgungstechnologien die auf ihren gerten abgelegt werden es gibt vier arten von cookies die wir mglicherweise verwenden absolut notwendige cookies sind notwendig damit unsere honeywellprivacyhoneywellcom actualizado 11 de junio de 2021 este aviso de cookies describe cmo honeywell international inc y sus afiliados conjuntamente honeywell nos o nosotros utilizan cookies y tecnologas similares instaladas en dispositivos como ordenadores mviles o tabletas dispositivos de los visitantes o usuarios de nuestra pgina web productos yo aplicaciones sitios las cookies y las tecnologas similares pueden procesar informacin personal consulte nuestra declaracin de privacidad si quiere obtener ms informacin sobre cmo procesamos su informacin personal y cmo ejercer sus derechos como persona interesada nuestro centro de preferencias de privacidad para obtener ms informacin sobre las cookies especficas que utilizamos en nuestros sitios con el fin de gestionar sus preferencias de cookies qu son las cookies las cookies son pequeos archivos de texto que nuestros sitios colocan en sus dispositivos cuando vuelve a visitar nuestros sitios nuestras tecnologas se conectan automticamente con la cookie para identificarlo a usted o a su dispositivo y recordar su informacin como sus preferencias de idioma o su informacin de acceso tambin utilizamos cookies de terceros que son cookies de un dominio distinto al dominio que usted est visitando lo que nos permite a nosotros al tercero que posee las cookies y en algunos casos a otros participantes en redes de cookies identificarlo a usted o a su dispositivo al visitar distintas pginas web con la palabra cookies nos referimos a fragmentos de texto pxeles gifs transparentes archivos de registro contadores de visitantes u otras tecnologas similares de seguimiento que se colocan en su dispositivo hay cuatro tipos de cookies que podemos utilizar cookies estrictamente necesarias que son requeridas por nuestros sitios para poder funcionar y proporcionarle los servicios e informacin que ha solicitado las cookies estrictamente necesarias estn exentas del requisito de consentimiento cookies funcionales que permiten una funcionalidad y personalizacin mejoradas por ejemplo permiten que nuestros sitios recuerden informacin que nos proporciona como sus preferencias de idioma y que almacenen informacin til para sus interacciones con nuestros sitios las podemos establecer nosotros o los proveedores externos cuyos servicios hemos aadido a nuestros sitios si no acepta estas cookies puede que todos o algunos de estos servicios no funcionen correctamente cookies de rendimiento que recogen informacin sobre el uso que hace de nuestros sitios p ej nos permiten contabilizar las visitas y las fuentes de trfico y nos ayudan a descubrir cmo funcionan nuestros sitios para poder realizar las mejoras pertinentes que podran aumentar su experiencia de navegacin p ej nos permiten saber qu pginas son las ms y menos populares toda la informacin que recopilan estas cookies es colectiva y por lo tanto annima cookies de publicidadsegmentacin que recogen datos sobre su actividad en lnea e identifican sus intereses para que podamos crear un perfil para usted y proporcionarle anuncios ms relevantes tambin realizan acciones como prevenir que siempre le aparezcan los mismos anuncios asegurar que los anuncios se muestran correctamente y seleccionar anuncios basados en sus intereses para obtener ms informacin sobre las cookies que honeywell utiliza visite nuestro centro de preferencias de privacidad por qu utilizamos cookies y otras tecnologas similares utilizamos cookies y otras tecnologas similares de seguimiento para los siguientes propsitos guardar sus preferencias y configuracin permitir que inicie sesin y se autentique para que pueda acceder a nuestros sitios y se pueda mover entre pginas dentro de nuestros sitios proteger nuestros sitios incluidas la deteccin y la prevencin de fraudes adaptar la informacin que se le presenta en funcin de sus preferencias de navegacin como el idioma y la regin geogrfica monitorizar los patrones de trfico de los usuarios dentro de nuestros navegacin y ofrecer servicios que sean ms relevantes para usted proveernos de informacin comercial y de marketing rastrear a los usuarios que visitan interactan o utilizan cualquiera de nuestros bizimle aadaki adresten iletiim kurun honeywellprivacyhoneywellcom english updated june 11 2021 this cookie notice describes how honeywell international inc and its affiliates collectively honeywell us or we use cookies and similar technologies installed on devices such as a computer mobile device or tablet devices of the visitors to or users of our website products andor applications sites cookies and similar technologies may process personal information please visit our privacy statement if you want to obtain more information about how we process your personal information and how to exercise your data subject rights our privacy preference center for more information on the specific cookies we use on our sites and to manage your cookie preferences what are cookies cookies are small text files that our sites place on your devices when you revisit our sites our technologies connect automatically with the cookie to identify you or your device and recall information about you such as your language preference or login information we also use thirdparty cookies which are cookies from a domain different than the domain of the website you are visiting which allow us the third party that owns the cookies and in some cases other participants in cookie networks to identify you or your device as you visit different websites we use the word cookies to include a piece of text pixels clear gifs log files web beacons or other similar tracking technology that are placed on your devices there are four types of cookies that we may use strictly necessary cookies are needed for our sites to function and to provide you with the services and information that you have requested strictly necessary cookies are exempt from the consent requirement functional cookies enable enhanced functionality and personalisation for example they allow our sites to remember information that you provide such as your language preferences and to store technical information useful for your interactions with our sites they may be set by us or by thirdparty providers whose services we have added to our sites if you do not allow these cookies then some or all of these services may not function properly performance cookies collect information about your use of our sites for eg it allows us to count visits and traffic sources and help us learn how our sites are performing so that we can make relevant improvements that could better your browsing experience for eg it allow us to know which pages are the most and least popular all information these cookies collect is aggregated and therefore anonymous advertising targeting cookies collect data about your online activity and identify your interests so that we can create a profile for you and to provide advertising that is more relevant to you they also perform functions like preventing the same adverts from continuously reappearing ensuring that adverts are properly displayed and selecting adverts that are based on your interests for more information on the cookies that honeywell uses please visit our privacy preference center why do we use cookies and other similar technologies we use cookies and other similar tracking technologies for the following purposes store your preferences and settings permit you to signin and authenticate you so that you can access our sites and to move from page to page within our sites secure our sites including fraud detection and prevention tailor information presented to you based on your browsing preferences such as language and geographical region monitor the traffic patterns of users within our sites and to collect statistics regarding your website usage to help us understand how our sites perform and how we can improve our sites for purposes such as enhancing your browsing experience and offering services that are more relevant to you provide us with business and marketing information track users who visit interact with or use any of our sites social media pages online advertisements and marketing communications such as which adverts where clicked on or if a user has opened or forwarded an email we have sent them and targeted advertising and crossdevice and crosssite tracking who uses the information stored in cookies and similar tracking technologies the information stored in our sites cookies is used exclusively by us or by third parties acting on our behalf with the exception of thirdparty cookies which are used and managed by external parties to provide services requested by us to improve our services and your experience when navigating our sites for more information on the firstparty and thirdparty cookies that honeywell uses please visit our privacy preference center what about flash cookies or local shared objects we may use flash cookies or local shared objects flash lsos to store your website preferences personalise your visit prevent fraud and for other site operations if you do not want flash lsos stored on your computer you can adjust the settings of your flash player to block flash lsos storage using the tools contained in the website storage settings panel you can also control flash lsos by going to the global storage settings panel and following the instructions which may include instructions that explain for example how to delete existing flash lsos targeted advertising we track and analyse both individualized usage and aggregated statistical information related to your use of our sites we also partner with third parties such as advertisers and ad partners to display advertising on our sites and to manage and serve advertising on other thirdparty sites these third parties use cookies and similar tracking technologies to collect and use certain information about your online activities either on our sites or other thirdparty sites to measure and track the effectiveness of advertisements and our online marketing activities for example by collecting data on how many times you click on one of our advertisements this information may be used alone or in combination with information about you we obtain from other sources like our data partners your contact details and honeywell transaction history to infer your interests and deliver you targeted advertisements and marketing that are more tailored to you based on your browsing activities and inferred interests interestbased advertising such interestbased advertising will only be delivered where permitted by applicable law and in accordance with your advertisingmarketing preferences please note that other third parties cookies and technologies are governed by each companys specific privacy policy and not this cookie notice crossdevice and crosssite tracking we our service providers and other third parties such as google and other ad partners may use information we collect about you whether directly from our sites or from a third party for the purposes of recognizing you online by identifying the devices that you use we use this information to serve you targeted advertising across multiple different devices crossdevice matching and sites crosssite tracking crossdevice matching and crosssite tracking allows us to better understand our customers activity improve our ability to target and measure ad campaigns including limiting the number of times a user sees an advert it also helps us match devices so we can facilitate your optout choices across all the devices we know are connected to an optedout cookie disabling cookies and opting out of interestbased advertising you can make choices about receiving cookies by using our privacy preference center or alternatively your browser settings should allow you to delete andor disable website cookies for more information about how to delete your cookies in your web browser refer to your browsers instructions google chrome internet explorer microsoft edge mozilla firefox opera safari mac iphone ipad or ipod touch if you choose to disable cookies you may find sites may not work in the same way some cookies are necessary to record and respect the choices you have made in regard to not being contacted or to not have other types of cookies added to your device if you delete cookies from your computer the cookie used to recognize your preferences including interestbased advertising will also be deleted requiring you to make your choices again users may also opt out of thirdparty ad networks through the use of various trade association websites such as network advertising initiative nai httpwwwnetworkadvertisingorgchoices digital advertising alliance daa i global httpsoptoutaboutadsinfo ii europe httpyouronlinechoiceseu opting out of interestbased advertising will opt you out from these companies delivery of interestbased content or ads to you but does not mean you no longer will receive any advertising through our website or other websites you may still see honeywell ads but those ads will not be customized to you by honeywell or our partners if at any time you do not want your personal information to be used to allow thirdparties to display advertisements or to personalize advertisements displayed to you you may also adjust your settings by using the tools provided by thirdparties such as google facebook and linkedin do not track dnt some web browsers may transmit donottrack signals to sites with which you communicate unsere technologien automatisch eine verbindung mit dem cookie her um sie oder ihr gert zu identifizieren und informationen zu ihnen abzurufen z b ihre spracheinstellungen oder anmeldeinformationen transparente gifs protokolldateien webbeacons oder andere hnliche nachverfolgungstechnologien die auf ihren gerten abgelegt werden es gibt vier arten von cookies die wir mglicherweise verwenden absolut notwendige cookies sind notwendig damit unsere websites funktionieren und wir ihnen die angeforderten services und informationen bereitstellen knnen absolut notwendige cookies sind von der descrive come honeywell international inc e le sue affiliate collettivamente honeywell nostro o noi utilizzano cookie e tecnologie assimilabili installati su dispositivi quali computer dispositivi mobili o tablet dispositivi dei visitatori o degli utenti del nostro sito web dei nostri prodotti eo applicazioni siti cookie e tecnologie assimilabili possono elaborare informazioni personali vi invitiamo a prendere visione di quanto segue la nostra informativa sulla privacy se desidera ricevere maggiori informazioni su come trattiamo le informazioni personali dellutente e su come esercitare i propri diritti in materia di dati personali il nostro centro preferenze sulla privacy per maggiori informazioni sui cookie specifici che utilizziamo sui nostri siti e per gestire le preferenze relative ai cookie cosa sono i cookie i cookie sono piccoli file di testo che i nostri siti inviano e registrano nei dispositivi degli utenti quando lutente visita nuovamente i nostri siti le nostre tecnologie si collegano automaticamente al cookie per identificare lutente o il suo dispositivo e richiamare informazioni sullutente come la preferenza della lingua o le informazioni di accesso utilizziamo anche cookie di terze parti che sono cookie di un dominio diverso da quello del sito web che lutente sta visitando e che permettono a noi alla terza parte proprietaria dei cookie e in alcuni casi ad altri partecipanti alle reti di cookie di identificare lutente o il suo dispositivo mentre visita diversi siti web utilizziamo la parola cookie per includere un pezzo di testo pixel clear gif file di log web beacon o altre tecnologie di tracciamento simili che sono installate sui dispositivi dellutente esistono quattro tipi di cookie che possiamo utilizzare i cookie strettamente necessari sono essenziali per il funzionamento dei nostri siti e per fornire allutente i servizi e le informazioni che ha richiesto i cookie strettamente necessari non richiedono alcun consenso i cookie funzionali permettono una maggiore funzionalit e personalizzazione per esempio consentono ai nostri siti di ricordare le informazioni fornite dallutente come le preferenze di lingua e di memorizzare informazioni tecniche utili per linterazione con i nostri siti possono essere impostati da noi o da fornitori terzi i cui servizi siano stati aggiunti ai nostri siti se non si accettano questi cookie alcuni o tutti questi servizi potrebbero non funzionare correttamente i cookie di prestazione acquisiscono informazioni sullutilizzo dei nostri siti per esempio ci consentono di contare il numero di visitatori e le fonti di traffico e ci aiutano a conoscere le prestazioni dei nostri siti in modo da poter apportare miglioramenti rilevanti che potrebbero ottimizzare lesperienza di navigazione degli utenti per esempio ci consentono di sapere quali siano le pagine pi e quali le meno apprezzate tutte le informazioni acquisite da questi cookie sono aggregate e quindi anonime i cookie pubblicitaridi profilazione acquisiscono dati sullattivit online dellutente e identificano i suoi interessi in modo da poter creare un profilo dellutente e fornire una pubblicit pi mirata svolgono anche funzioni come evitare che gli stessi annunci riappaiano continuamente garantire la corretta visualizzazione degli annunci e selezionare gli annunci in base agli interessi dellutente per wij gebruikmaken van cookies en vergelijkbare technologien die zijn genstalleerd op apparaten zoals computers mobiele apparaten of tablets apparaten van bezoekers aan of gebruikers van onze website technologien automatisch met de cookie om u of uw apparaat te identificeren en informatie over u op te roepen zoals uw taalvoorkeur of aanmeldgegevens we gebruiken ook cookies van derden dit zijn voorzien van de door u verzochte diensten en informatie strikt noodzakelijke cookies zijn vrijgesteld van de toestemmingsvereiste functionele cookies maken verbeterde functionaliteit en personalisatie de cookies describe cmo honeywell international inc y sus afiliados conjuntamente honeywell nos o nosotros utilizan cookies y tecnologas similares instaladas en dispositivos como ordenadores mviles o tabletas dispositivos de los visitantes o usuarios de nuestra pgina web productos yo aplicaciones sitios las cookies y las tecnologas similares pueden procesar informacin personal consulte nuestra declaracin de privacidad si quiere obtener ms informacin sobre cmo procesamos su informacin personal y cmo ejercer sus derechos como persona interesada nuestro centro de preferencias de privacidad para obtener ms informacin sobre las cookies especficas que utilizamos en nuestros sitios con el fin de gestionar sus preferencias de cookies qu son las cookies las cookies son pequeos archivos de texto que nuestros sitios colocan en sus dispositivos cuando vuelve a visitar nuestros sitios nuestras tecnologas se conectan automticamente con la cookie para identificarlo a usted o a su dispositivo y recordar su informacin como sus preferencias de idioma o su informacin de acceso tambin utilizamos cookies de terceros que son cookies de un dominio distinto al dominio que usted est visitando lo que nos permite a nosotros al tercero que posee las cookies y en algunos casos a otros participantes en redes de cookies identificarlo a usted o a su dispositivo al visitar distintas pginas web con la palabra cookies nos referimos a fragmentos de texto pxeles gifs transparentes archivos de registro contadores de visitantes u otras tecnologas similares de seguimiento que se colocan en su dispositivo hay cuatro tipos de cookies que podemos utilizar cookies estrictamente necesarias que son requeridas por nuestros sitios para poder funcionar y proporcionarle los servicios e informacin que ha solicitado las cookies estrictamente necesarias estn exentas del requisito de consentimiento cookies funcionales que permiten una funcionalidad y personalizacin mejoradas por ejemplo permiten que nuestros sitios recuerden informacin que nos proporciona como sus preferencias de idioma y que almacenen informacin til para sus interacciones con nuestros sitios las podemos establecer nosotros o los proveedores externos cuyos servicios hemos aadido a nuestros sitios si no acepta estas cookies puede que todos o algunos de estos servicios no funcionen correctamente cookies de rendimiento que recogen informacin sobre el uso que hace de nuestros sitios p ej nos permiten contabilizar las visitas y las fuentes de trfico y nos ayudan a descubrir cmo funcionan nuestros sitios para poder realizar las mejoras pertinentes que podran aumentar su experiencia de navegacin p ej nos permiten saber qu pginas son las ms y menos populares toda la informacin que recopilan estas cookies es colectiva y por lo tanto annima cookies de publicidadsegmentacin que recogen datos sobre su actividad en lnea e identifican sus intereses para que podamos crear un perfil para usted y proporcionarle anuncios ms relevantes tambin realizan acciones como prevenir que siempre le aparezcan los mismos anuncios asegurar que los anuncios se muestran correctamente y seleccionar anuncios basados en sus intereses para obtener ms informacin sobre las cookies que honeywell utiliza visite nuestro centro de preferencias de privacidad por qu utilizamos cookies y otras tecnologas similares utilizamos cookies y otras tecnologas similares de seguimiento para los siguientes propsitos guardar sus preferencias y configuracin permitir que inicie sesin y se autentique para que pueda acceder a nuestros sitios y se pueda mover entre pginas dentro de nuestros sitios proteger nuestros sitios incluidas la deteccin y la prevencin de fraudes adaptar la informacin que se le presenta en funcin de sus preferencias de navegacin como el idioma y la regin geogrfica monitorizar los patrones de trfico de los usuarios dentro de nuestros sitios y recopilar estadsticas sobre el uso que dan a la pgina web para ayudarnos a comprender cmo responden nuestros sitios y cmo podemos mejorarlos para por ejemplo aumentar su experiencia de navegacin y ofrecer servicios que sean ms relevantes para usted proveernos de informacin comercial y de marketing rastrear a los usuarios que visitan interactan o utilizan cualquiera de nuestros sitios pginas de redes sociales anuncios en lnea y comunicaciones de marketing como en qu anuncios hizo clic o si un usuario ha abierto o reenviado un correo electrnico que le hemos enviado publicidad dirigida y seguimiento cruzado entre dispositivos y entre pginas web en las cookies de nuestros sitios con la excepcin de las cookies de terceros que las utilizan y gestionan terceros para proporcionar servicios solicitados por nosotros a fin de mejorar nuestros
